}\n92: \n93:   // The WithAck version first calls the ack-less version, then adds in the passed-in ack.\n94:   // Returns a new'd pointer, meant to be owned by the caller, who is expected to know what type the\n95:   // pointer actually is.\n96:   std::unique_ptr<RQ> getNextRequestWithAck(const UpdateAck& ack) {\n97:     auto request = getNextRequestInternal();\n98:     request->set_response_nonce(ack.nonce_);\n99:     ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"ACK for {} will have nonce {}\", typeUrl(), ack.nonce_);\n100:     if (ack.error_detail_.code() != Grpc::Status::WellKnownGrpcStatus::Ok) {\n101:       // Don't needlessly make the field present-but-empty if status is ok.\n102:       request->mutable_error_detail()->CopyFrom(ack.error_detail_);\n103:     }\n104:     return request;\n105:   }\n106: \n107:   virtual void ttlExpiryCallback(const std::vector<std::string>& type_url) PURE;\n108: \n109: protected:\n110:   virtual std::unique_ptr<RQ> getNextRequestInternal() PURE;\n111:   virtual void handleGoodResponse(const RS& message) PURE;\n112:   void handleBadResponse(const EnvoyException& e, UpdateAck& ack) {\n113:     // Note that error_detail being set is what indicates that a (Delta)DiscoveryRequest is a NACK.\n114:     ack.error_detail_.set_code(Grpc::Status::WellKnownGrpcStatus::Internal);\n115:     ack.error_detail_.set_message(Config::Utility::truncateGrpcStatusMessage(e.what()));\n116:     ENVOY_LOG(warn, \"Config for {} rejected: {}\", typeUrl(), e.what());\n117:     callbacks().onConfigUpdateFailed(Envoy::Config::ConfigUpdateFailureReason::UpdateRejected, &e);\n118:   }\n119: \n120:   std::string typeUrl() const { return type_url_; Let me compile my findings:\n\n## Key Components Found:\n\n### 1. **Unified Template-based Architecture (XdsMux namespace)**\n- **GrpcMuxImpl<S, F, RQ, RS>** template (xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h) - The unified template that supports both SotW and Delta variants\n- **GrpcMuxSotw** - Concrete specialization for State-of-the-World (SotW) using DiscoveryRequest/Response\n- **GrpcMuxDelta** - Concrete specialization for Delta using DeltaDiscoveryRequest/Response\n- **NullGrpcMuxImpl** - Placeholder when no ADS is configured\n\n### 2. **Subscription State Management (XdsMux namespace)**\n- **BaseSubscriptionState<RS, RQ>** template (xds_mux/subscription_state.h) - Abstract parent class for protocol state\n- **SotwSubscriptionState** (xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.h) - Tracks SotW protocol state for each type_url\n- **SotwSubscriptionStateFactory** - Factory for creating SotwSubscriptionState instances\n- **DeltaSubscriptionState** (xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.h) - Tracks Delta protocol state for each type_url\n- **DeltaSubscriptionStateFactory** - Factory for creating DeltaSubscriptionState instances\n\n### 3. **Adapter Layer**\n- **GrpcSubscriptionImpl** (grpc_subscription_impl.h) - Adapter from typed Subscription to untyped GrpcMux\n- **GrpcCollectionSubscriptionImpl** - Specialization for collection-based subscriptions\n\n### 4. **Factory for Selecting Between Modes**\n\n\n- **GrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory** (grpc_subscription_factory.h) - Creates SotW subscriptions\n- **DeltaGrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory** - Creates Delta subscriptions\n- **AdsConfigSubscriptionFactory** - Creates subscriptions using ADS mux\n- A runtime feature flag \"envoy.reloadable_features.unified_mux\" determines whether to use the unified implementations (GrpcMuxSotw/GrpcMuxDelta) or the legacy ones (GrpcMuxImpl/NewGrpcMuxImpl)\n\n### 5. **Legacy Implementations** (Being deprecated)\n- **GrpcMuxImpl** (grpc_m ux_impl.h) - Legacy SotW implementation\n-
